***aftroggelen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aftroggelen.html>aftroggelen</a> (55163)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:af.html>af</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">troggelen</i>, the second part <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">truggelen</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">troggelen</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aftroggelen.html>aftroggelen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> with optional indirect object</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to unfairly obtain through smooth talking, insisting, pleading etc.; to cadge
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">"<a href = vnd.unilang:gij.html>Gij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zoudt.html>zoudt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>u</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nog.html>nog</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uw.html>uw</a> eerstgeboorterecht <a href = vnd.unilang:laten.html>laten</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:aftroggelen.html>aftroggelen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:schotel.html>schotel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:linzen.html>linzen</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:gij.html>gij</a>!"</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">"You would <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> let yourself <b>be tricked out</b> of your primogeniture for a dish of lentils, you!"</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">afhandig <a href = vnd.unilang:maken.html>maken</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:afval.html>afval</a></i>, shortening of <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">slachtafval</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">that which fell off from slaughtered meat.</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:af.html>af</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:val.html>val</a></i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">offal</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:afvallen.html>afvallen</a> (11520)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:afvallen.html>afvallen</a></i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:af.html>af</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vallen.html>vallen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:afvallen.html>afvallen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fall off</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to lose weight, <a href = vnd.unilang:slim.html>slim</a> down</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to drop out, to no longer be able to partake</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to renounce, to renege, to lose loyalty</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to dispute, to go against (a person)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:afwenden.html>afwenden</a> (35368)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:afwenden.html>afwenden</a></i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:af.html>af</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wenden.html>wenden</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:afwenden.html>afwenden</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to stave off, to avert, to obviate, to prevent
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:onheil.html>onheil</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werd.html>werd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:toedoen.html>toedoen</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:afwenden.html>afgewend</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The misfortune <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <b>prevented</b> through her efforts.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">reflexive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to turn away</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:afwerken.html>afwerken</a> (14473)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:af.html>af</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:werken.html>werken</a></i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:afwerken.html>afwerken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to finish, to complete work on</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to finish work for the day</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***afzetten.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:afzetten.html>afzetten</a> (4029)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">afsetten</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:af.html>af</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zetten.html>zetten</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:afzetten.html>afzetten</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to take off (an item of clothing)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoed.html>hoed</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:afzetten.html>afzetten</a></b></i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">to <b>take off</b> a hat</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to switch off (an electronic device)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to amputate</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to demarcate, mark out with boundaries</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to sell (products or commodities, typically at a specific sales market)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to close off, to barricade (a street)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to dethrone, to remove from office</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to scam, to rip off</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to sediment, to deposit</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to drop off (a passenger at a destination)</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">afsweren</i>.
